<h1 class="DDPage__header-title">Lucy Burns Museum </h1>
<div class="DDPage__header-place-info">
<div class="DDPage__header-place-location"><a title="See all things to do in Lorton, Virginia." href="/things-to-do/lorton-virginia">Lorton, Virginia</a></div>
</div>
<h3 class="DDPage__header-dek">Located at the former Lorton Prison the Lucy Burns Museum tells the story of the 91 year history of the prison including the dark chapter of its involvement in the women&#39;s suffrage movement. &nbsp;</h3>
</div>

<div class="DDPage__left-rail grid-col-lg-2 grid-hide-md grid-hide-sm">
<div class="DDPDestinationInset hidden-print">
<div class="DDPDestinationInset__heading">Top Places in Lorton</div>

<img data-src="https://img.atlasobscura.com/QgJHCEuUVtmt0B6OV_MF4CGHJBkOUvwpe0Bn78LUe_A/rs:fill:372:248:1/g:ce/q:81/sm:1/scp:1/ar:1/aHR0cHM6Ly9hdGxh/cy1kZXYuczMuYW1h/em9uYXdzLmNvbS91/cGxvYWRzL3BsYWNl/X2ltYWdlcy83YzNl/ZWY2ZS03MThhLTQ2/NDgtOWExZS01N2I1/YTQ2M2FhNjQ1NTM1/ZGFhZDkyYTI0Yjkw/MjhfMkQyRDREN0Et/Mjc1Qy00NTVFLTkw/MkItRTc3MjNBMzhB/MzdELmpwZWc.jpg" alt="Stoney Lonesome Cemetery, 2019." data-width="4032" data-height="3024" class="lazy img-responsive DDPDestinationInset__image" nopin="nopin" src="https://assets.atlasobscura.com/assets/blank-11b9c95a68e295dddd0ea924647536578ce285b2c8469a223c01df1ff3166af1.png" />
</figure>
<div class="DDPDestinationInset__place">

</div>
</a>
<hr class="DDPDestinationInset__hr">

<div class="DDPDestinationInset__title">George Mason&#39;s Gunston Hall </div>
<div class="DDPDestinationInset__location">Lorton, Virginia</div>
</div>
</a>
<a href="/things-to-do/lorton-virginia" class="TextCTA--v2 DDPDestinationInset__see-all-link">See All <i class=" atlas-svg-wrap wrap-icon-aoc-arrow-forward">
<svg version="1.1" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink">
<use href="#icon-aoc-arrow-forward" xlink:href="#icon-aoc-arrow-forward" />
</svg>
</i>
</a>
</div>
</div>
<div class="DDPageContent__column grid-col-lg-6 grid-col-md-7">
<div id="place-body" class="DDP__body-copy">
<div>
<p><span class="section-start-text">Located just south of </span><a class="destination-link place-destination-link" href="/things-to-do/washington-dc"><span class="section-start-text">Washington</span></a><span class="section-start-text">,</span> D.C., this former workhouse prison by the Occoquan River was opened in 1910, commissioned by President Theodore Roosevelt to be more humane than its contemporary prisons. Yet the most notable chapter in its history is one of horrible treatment of the suffragists who were imprisoned here during the First World War, culminating in a “Night of Terror” that ended up being a turning point in the women’s movement.</p>
<p>Beginning in January of 1917, members of the National Woman’s Party began silently picketing for women’s suffrage every day in front of the White House. Initially the protest drew little attention and the picketers were seen as an interesting local curiosity. Gawking at the sign-bearing suffragists became something of a tourist stop for visitors to the nation’s capital. When President Woodrow Wilson left the White House in his limo, he would occasionally tip his hat and smile at the protesters, but otherwise ignored them.</p>
<p>However, the public’s detached attitude toward the picketers ended after only a few months after the United States entered World War 1, in April of 1917. The party decided to continue their protest during the fighting. This enraged some in the public and media, and the daily protests began to get more national attention. Capitalizing on the newfound media focus, the protesters made signs criticizing President Wilson’s hypocrisy for making speeches calling for democracy in Europe while it was lacking at home, and even referred to him as “Kaiser Wilson.”</p>
<p>In June of 1917, the police crackdown of the protesters began. Protesters were arrested for “obstructing traffic” and sentenced to upwards of 60 days in jail. Most of the women arrested were sent to the Occoquan Workhouse in <a class="destination-link place-destination-link" href="/things-to-do/virginia">Virginia</a>. The conditions were deplorable. All prisoners at Occoquan were forced to share a single bar of soap. They were served meals of rancid meat, moldy bread, and oatmeal in which they frequently found worms. Protesting the conditions at Occoquan, the suffragists began a hunger strike and prison guards began force feeding the prisoners a slurry of raw eggs and milk using funnels and tubes inserted up the nose.</p>
<p>The climax of the abuse occurred on November 14, 1917, in an event remembered as the “Night of Terror.” Frustrated with the defiance of the suffragist prisoners, the prison superintendent ordered his guards to brutally crack down on them. Suffragist Lucy Burns had her hands chained together over her head and was left dangling by her arms overnight. Another prisoner, Dora Lewis, was thrown against an iron bed and knocked unconscious. Lewis’s cellmate, thinking that Lewis had died, had a heart attack. Other suffragists were dragged, beaten, choked, and kicked.</p>
<p>Although the public was initially opposed to the protesters for continuing their picketing during wartime, they were horrified when they heard of the events of the Night of Terror. By November 28th, all of the imprisoned suffragists were released, and they vowed to continue their daily protest in front of the White House. Public pressure in favor of women’s suffrage grew and on January 9, 1918, President Wilson finally came out in favor of a constitutional amendment granting the vote to women.</p>
<p>The Occoquan Workhouse, later renamed the Lorton Reformatory, was closed in 2001 and the property was sold back to Fairfax County, Virginia. The facility was added to the National Register of Historic Places in 2006 and today the Workhouse Arts Center operates out of the former prison, with former prison blocks and cells converted into art studios and classrooms. They maintain a small museum to the facility’s former use, with special focus on the imprisoned suffragists and the Night of Terror.</p>
</div>
</div>
<div class="DDP__direction-copy">
<h6 class="DDPage__body-heading">Know Before You Go</h6>
<p><p>The Lucy Burns Museum is located in building W-2 and open Friday from 12 PM to 5 PM, 11am -5pm Saturday and Sunday from 12 PM - 5 PM. Admission is free for the main gallery and $5 per person to tour the cell block.  </p></p>
</div>

<div class="HorizontalCardWrapper --ExperienceSeriesWrapper ">
<a class="HorizontalCard js-link-tracked o-vertical-push-5" data-category="Cross Promotion Module" data-label="Place Main Column" data-action="Experience" href="/experiences/the-spies-of-georgetown">
<div class="HorizontalCard__content-wrap">
<div class="HorizontalCard__hat">Atlas Obscura Experiences</div>
<h3 class="HorizontalCard__heading">
<span class="js-socket-title">The Spies of Georgetown</span>

            window.AtlasObscura.randomPlaceModule.init();
            window.AtlasObscura.scrollEventsModule.addScrollFunction(function () {
              if (!isElementInViewport($('.navbar-main')) && window.AtlasObscura.randomPlaceModule.isActive()) {
                window.AtlasObscura.randomPlaceModule.showUI();
              }
            });
          }
        });
      </script>
<script>
        $(function() {
          function initBTE(selector) {
            $(selector + ' .vue-js-card-been-count,' + selector +' .vue-js-card-wanted-count').each(function (i, el) {
              new Vue({ el: el });
              $(el).removeClass('hidden');
            });
          }

          function initTooltips () {
            $("[data-toggle='tooltip']").tooltip();
          }

          function initControls () {
            $('.js-paginate-content-modal-controls').show();
            $('.js-paginate-content-modal-controls .js-modal-close-button').one('click', function() {
              $('.js-paginate-content-modal').modal('hide');
            })
          }

          function hideControls() {
            $('.js-paginate-content-modal-controls').hide();
          }

          $('.js-paginate-content-modal').on('shown.bs.modal', initControls);
          $('.js-paginate-content-modal').on('hide.bs.modal', hideControls);

          $('.js-see-all-link').click(function(){
            if($(this).data('loaded')) {
              $('.js-paginate-content-modal').modal('show');
            } else if ($(this).data('loading')) {
              return;
            } else {
              $('.js-see-all-link').data('loading', true);
              $.ajax({
                url: '/payloads/lists_for_place/' + $(this).data("placeId"),
              }).done(function(response){
                $('.js-see-all-link').data('loaded', true);
                $('.js-see-all-link').data('loading', false);
                $('.js-paginate-content-modal').find('.modal-body').append(response);
                $('.js-paginate-content-modal').modal('show');
                initTooltips();

                if (AtlasObscura.current_user) {
                  initBTE('.js-paginate-content-modal')
                }

                $('.js-paginate-content-modal').on('click', '.list-recirc-paginator a', function(e){
                  e.preventDefault();
                  $.ajax({
                    url: e.target
                  }).done(function(response) {
                    $('.js-paginate-content-modal')
                      .find('.modal-body .see-all-lists-modal-content')
                      .replaceWith(response).end()
                      .scrollTop(0);
                      if (AtlasObscura.current_user) {
                        initBTE('.js-paginate-content-modal')
                      }
                      initTooltips();
                  })
                })
              })
            }
          })
        })
      </script>
<script charset="utf-8">
         $(function(){
            function showBanner (bannerMarkup) {
              $('.DDPage').prepend($(bannerMarkup));
            }
            showBanner('');
         });
        </script>
<script>
        htlbid.cmd.push(function() {
          removeAdSlotIfEmpty('Place_Page_Inline_Desktop', '.partner-content-video-wrap');
          removeAdSlotIfEmpty('Mobile_Place_Page_Inline', '.partner-content-video-wrap');
        });
      </script>
